\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01680}01680\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ variance\ is\ the\ average\ of\ the\ squared\ deviations\ from\ the\ mean,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01681}01681\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ i.e.,\ \ \`{}\`{}var\ =\ mean(abs(x\ -\/\ x.mean())**2)\`{}\`{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01682}01682\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01683}01683\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ mean\ is\ normally\ calculated\ as\ \`{}\`{}x.sum()\ /\ N\`{}\`{},\ where\ \`{}\`{}N\ =\ len(x)\`{}\`{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01684}01684\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ If,\ however,\ \`{}ddof\`{}\ is\ specified,\ the\ divisor\ \`{}\`{}N\ -\/\ ddof\`{}\`{}\ is\ used}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01685}01685\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ instead.\ \ In\ standard\ statistical\ practice,\ \`{}\`{}ddof=1\`{}\`{}\ provides\ an}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01686}01686\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ unbiased\ estimator\ of\ the\ variance\ of\ a\ hypothetical\ infinite}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01687}01687\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ population.\ \ \`{}\`{}ddof=0\`{}\`{}\ provides\ a\ maximum\ likelihood\ estimate\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01688}01688\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ variance\ for\ normally\ distributed\ variables.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01689}01689\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01690}01690\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Note\ that\ for\ complex\ numbers,\ the\ absolute\ value\ is\ taken\ before}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01691}01691\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ squaring,\ so\ that\ the\ result\ is\ always\ real\ and\ nonnegative.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01692}01692\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01693}01693\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ For\ floating-\/point\ input,\ the\ variance\ is\ computed\ using\ the\ same}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01694}01694\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ precision\ the\ input\ has.\ \ Depending\ on\ the\ input\ data,\ this\ can\ cause}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01695}01695\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ the\ results\ to\ be\ inaccurate,\ especially\ for\ \`{}float32\`{}\ (see\ example}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{nanfunctions_8py_source_l01696}01696\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ below).\ \ Specifying\ a\ higher-\/accuracy\ accumulator\ using\ the\ \`{}\`{}dtype\`{}\`{}}}
